            <h4 class="widget-title">
             New York Microscope Company Inc.
            </h4>
            <p>
             NY Microscope Co. is a full-service microscope company. We specialize in high-quality microscopes, digital microscopes and digital cameras offered at competitive prices. We service and repair all brands of microscopes, on the field or at our in-house service center. Whether you need to find a certain stereo microscope for your lab, classroom or industry, seek repair work for a damaged light microscope, or can't find a specific microscope part, NY Microscope Co. can provide the necessary solution.
            </p>
